52:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Conclusion"}]
53:["$","p",null,{"children":"We showed that the Kalman filter can be recovered using basic probability tools & the Woodbury matrix identity. The main assumption we made is that state belief, observation noise, and evolution uncertainty are Gaussian. These assumptions make computations simpler, but the same base principles can be used without these assumptions to handle cases where a richer modelisation is needed. However, these alternative algorithms are often more computationally costly."}]

&\qquad+ \v{K}\v{o} \\
&= \v{\mu} + \v{K}(\v{o} - \v{M}\v{\mu})
